# Ask Combination Audit

**Review basis only.** This report is generated for Philipp/Cowork curation review; it is not a frontend data source.

- Command: `npm run audit:ask-combinations`
- Question source: `src/lib/ask/questions.ts`
- Recommender: `src/lib/ask/recommend.ts`
- Combinations: 225
- Recommendation limit per combination: Top-10
- Weak-score threshold: top score < 35
- Markdown: `C:\Users\Phil\chrono-lexicanum-product\ingest\ask\audit-ask-combinations.md`
- JSON detail: `C:\Users\Phil\chrono-lexicanum-product\ingest\ask\audit-ask-combinations.json`

## Curation reference frame

- FanFiAddict beginner guide: https://fanfiaddict.com/so-you-want-to-start-reading-warhammer-40000-heres-where-to-start/
- WH40K Book Club beginner guide: https://wh40kbookclub.com/beginners-guide-to-warhammer-40000/
- Lane-scoped anchors (`scripts/seed-data/ask-anchors.json`) seed the canonical entry per slice: Eisenhorn/Vaults of Terra (Imperium-investigative), Gaunt/Cain/Cadia (Imperium-military), Space Wolf/Brothers of the Snake (loyalist SM), Night Lords/Soul Hunter (heretic-grimdark), The Infinite and the Divine (xenos), Horus Rising (heretic + experience=some).

## Gate verification

- **HH gate (newcomer):** 0.0% of newcomer Top-10 slots are Horus-Heresy books (0/750). Must be 0.
- **Deep gate (anchors):** 0.0% of deep Top-10 slots are anchor books (0/750). Must be 0.
- Context — some/deep Heresy exposure: 9.0% (135/1500 slots); no gate, the Heresy is allowed once you're past newcomer.

## Tone distinctness

Tone is the dominant axis (Brief 164): holding experience/faction/length fixed, each of the four concrete tones should yield a distinct #1. **32/36** contexts give four distinct tone champions. Informational, not a hard gate.

Accepted structural exceptions — one book legitimately owns two registers in a narrow pool, and forcing a split would promote a worse #1:

| Context (experience / faction / length) | Book | Tones sharing #1 |
|---|---|---|
| new / imperium_of_man / trilogy | Xenos | grimdark, investigative |
| some / imperium_of_man / trilogy | Xenos | grimdark, investigative |
| deep / imperium_of_man / trilogy | Ravenor: The Omnibus | grimdark, heroic, investigative |
| deep / xenos / standalone | Long Live Da Red Gobbo | heroic, military |
